I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Language/role/version set in filename, e.g. mypage._role_member.md should replace any mount configuration for that dimension
This relates to #14750 -- of solving that issue has made this issue more visible.

If I have this `roles` and `mounts` config:

```toml
[roles]
    [roles.guest]
        weight = 100
    [roles.member]
        weight = 200

[module]
    [[module.mounts]]
        source = 'content/member'
        target = 'content'
        [module.mounts.sites.matrix]
            roles = "member"
    [[module.mounts]]
        source = 'content/guest'
        target = 'content'
        [module.mounts.sites.matrix]
            # This allows the member role to also see the guest content.
            # But note the order of the mounts here, this will be fallback content for members.
            roles = "*"
```

And this in `content/member`:

```
_index.md           20220330_094321.jpg 20220330_094357.jpg 20220330_095331.jpg
```

And this in `content/guest`:

```
_index.md                        20220330_094115._role_member_.jpg 20221020_114303.jpg
```

The current behavior for the bundled resource `20220330_094115._role_guest.jpg` in `content/member` is that:

* It gets assigned all roles from the mount config (`roles = "*"`)
* It gets assigned the `member` role from the filename.

The expected and obviously most useful behaviour would be if any dimension value(s) (language, role or version) in the filename would replace any existing file mount config for that dimension. In the example above `20220330_094115._role_member.jpg` would be assigned the `member` role only.

A note mostly to myself re the above: Any sites matrix definition in front matter will work how we want the filename to work above, to the order of precedence after fixing this would be front matter => filename => file mount, which I think makes the most sense.  




</pr_description>

    40	        prefixVersion      = "version_"
    41	        prefixRole         = "role_"
    42	        prefixOutputFormat = "outputformat_"
    43	        prefixKind         = "kind_"
    44	        prefixLayout       = "layout_"

    47	// isCustomWrapperIdentifier tells whether a supplied path is of the form _xyz_.
    48	// must have non-empty content between the identifierCustomWrapper's to pass.
    49	func isCustomWrapperIdentifier(s string) bool {
    50	        return len(s) > 2*len(identifierCustomWrapper) &&
    51	                strings.HasPrefix(s, identifierCustomWrapper) &&
    52	                strings.HasSuffix(s, identifierCustomWrapper)
    53	}
    54	
    55	// parsePrefixIdentifier parses inner content of a wrapper block (with outer underscores stripped)
    56	// and returns the prefix. The prefix match is case-insensitive.
    57	// Returns empty string if not a known prefix.
    58	func parsePrefixIdentifier(inner string) string {
    59	        innerLower := strings.ToLower(inner)
    60	        for _, p := range []string{prefixLanguage, prefixVersion, prefixRole, prefixOutputFormat, prefixKind, prefixLayout} {
    61	                if strings.HasPrefix(innerLower, p) {
    62	                        return p
    63	                }
    64	        }
    65	        return ""
    66	}
    67	
    68	// findWrapperDotPositions returns positions of dots inside ._..._. wrapper blocks.
    69	// These dots should be skipped during the main backward dot-scanning loop,
    70	// so that wrapper blocks are treated as single opaque segments.
    71	func findWrapperDotPositions(s string) []int {
    72	        lastSlash := strings.LastIndex(s, "/")
    73	        if lastSlash == -1 {
    74	                return nil
    75	        }
    76	
    77	        var skipDots []int
    78	        i := lastSlash
    79	        for i < len(s) {
    80	                // Look for ._ which could start a wrapper block.
    81	                if i+2 < len(s) && s[i] == '.' && s[i+1] == '_' {
    82	                        // Find the closing _. or _ at end of string.
    83	                        end := -1
    84	                        for j := i + 2; j < len(s); j++ {
    85	                                if s[j] == '/' {
    86	                                        break
    87	                                }
    88	                                if s[j] == '_' && (j+1 >= len(s) || s[j+1] == '.') {
    89	                                        end = j
    90	                                        break
    91	                                }
    92	                        }
    93	                        if end != -1 {
    94	                                // Record dot positions inside the wrapper block.
    95	                                for j := i + 2; j < end; j++ {
    96	                                        if s[j] == '.' {
    97	                                                skipDots = append(skipDots, j)
    98	                                        }
    99	                                }
   100	                                i = end + 1
   101	                                continue
   102	                        }
   103	                }
   104	                i++
   105	        }
   106	        return skipDots
   107	}
   108	
   109	// isSkippedDot reports whether position i is in the sorted skipDots slice.
   110	func isSkippedDot(skipDots []int, i int) bool {
   111	        for _, d := range skipDots {
   112	                if d == i {
   113	                        return true
   114	                }
   115	                if d > i {
   116	                        break
   117	                }
   118	        }
   119	        return false
   120	}
   121	
   122	// applyPrefixIdentifier validates and stores a prefix identifier.
   123	// id is the value-only LowHigh (e.g. pointing at "v1.0.0" in p.s, not the full wrapper).
   124	// Returns true if the identifier was recognized and applied.
   125	func (pp *PathParser) applyPrefixIdentifier(component, prefix string, p *Path, id types.LowHigh[string]) bool {
   126	        value := strings.ToLower(p.s[id.Low:id.High])
   127	        switch prefix {
   128	        case prefixLanguage:
   129	                if pp.LanguageIndex != nil {
   130	                        if _, ok := pp.LanguageIndex[value]; ok {
   131	                                p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   132	                                p.posIdentifierPrefixLanguages = append(p.posIdentifierPrefixLanguages, len(p.identifiersKnown)-1)
   133	                                return true
   134	                        }
   135	                        if pp.IsLangDisabled != nil && pp.IsLangDisabled(value) {
   136	                                p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   137	                                p.posIdentifierPrefixLanguages = append(p.posIdentifierPrefixLanguages, len(p.identifiersKnown)-1)
   138	                                p.disabled = true
   139	                                return true
   140	                        }
   141	                }
   142	        case prefixVersion:
   143	                if pp.ConfiguredDimensions != nil {
   144	                        if idx := pp.ConfiguredDimensions.ConfiguredVersions.ResolveIndex(value); idx >= 0 {
   145	                                p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   146	                                p.posIdentifierVersions = append(p.posIdentifierVersions, len(p.identifiersKnown)-1)
   147	                                return true
   148	                        }
   149	                }
   150	        case prefixRole:
   151	                if pp.ConfiguredDimensions != nil {
   152	                        if idx := pp.ConfiguredDimensions.ConfiguredRoles.ResolveIndex(value); idx >= 0 {
   153	                                p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   154	                                p.posIdentifierRoles = append(p.posIdentifierRoles, len(p.identifiersKnown)-1)
   155	                                return true
   156	                        }
   157	                }
   158	        case prefixOutputFormat:
   159	                if component == files.ComponentFolderLayouts && pp.IsOutputFormat != nil {
   160	                        if pp.IsOutputFormat(value, "") {
   161	                                p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   162	                                p.posIdentifierPrefixOutputFormat = len(p.identifiersKnown) - 1
   163	                                return true
   164	                        }
   165	                }
   166	        case prefixKind:
   167	                if component == files.ComponentFolderLayouts {
   168	                        if kinds.GetKindMain(value) != "" {
   169	                                p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   170	                                p.posIdentifierPrefixKind = len(p.identifiersKnown) - 1
   171	                                return true
   172	                        }
   173	                }
   174	        case prefixLayout:
   175	                if component == files.ComponentFolderLayouts {
   176	                        p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   177	                        p.posIdentifierPrefixLayout = len(p.identifiersKnown) - 1
   178	                        return true
   179	                }
   180	        }
   181	        return false
   182	}

   205	}
   206

   208	        pp.initOnce.Do(func() {
   209	                pp.sitesMatrixCache = hmaps.NewCache[string, sitesmatrix.VectorStore]()
   210	        })
   211	}

   652	        posIdentifierPrefixKind         int
   653	        posIdentifierPrefixLayout       int
   654	
   655	        // Name boundary, computed during parse.
   656	        posIdentifierName types.LowHigh[string]
   657	        // Position of the dot before the leftmost known identifier.
   658	        // Set during parseIdentifier, used to compute posIdentifierName.
   659	        posNameHigh int
   660	
   661	        disabled bool
   662	
   663	        trimLeadingSlash bool
   664	
   665	        unnormalized *Path
   666	}
   667	
   668	var pathPool = &sync.Pool{
   669	        New: func() any {
   670	                p := &Path{}
   671	                p.reset()
   672	                return p
   673	        },
   674	}
   675	
   676	func getPath() *Path {
   677	        return pathPool.Get().(*Path)
   678	}
   679	
   680	func putPath(p *Path) {
   681	        p.reset()
   682	        pathPool.Put(p)
   683	}
   684	
   685	func (p *Path) reset() {
   686	        p.s = ""
   687	        p.posContainerLow = -1
   688	        p.posContainerHigh = -1
   689	        p.posSectionHigh = -1
   690	        p.component = ""
   691	        p.pathType = 0
   692	        p.identifiersKnown = p.identifiersKnown[:0]
   693	        p.posIdentifierLanguage = -1
   694	        p.posIdentifierOutputFormat = -1
   695	        p.posIdentifierKind = -1
   696	        p.posIdentifierLayout = -1
   697	        p.posIdentifierBaseof = -1
   698	        p.posIdentifierCustom = -1
   699	        p.posIdentifierPrefixLanguages = p.posIdentifierPrefixLanguages[:0]
   700	        p.posIdentifierVersions = p.posIdentifierVersions[:0]
   701	        p.posIdentifierRoles = p.posIdentifierRoles[:0]
   702	        p.posIdentifierPrefixOutputFormat = -1
   703	        p.posIdentifierPrefixKind = -1
   704	        p.posIdentifierPrefixLayout = -1
   705	        p.posIdentifierName = types.LowHigh[string]{}
   706	        p.posNameHigh = -1
   707	        p.disabled = false
   708	        p.trimLeadingSlash = false
   709	        p.unnormalized = nil
   710	}
   711	
   712	// TrimLeadingSlash returns a copy of the Path with the leading slash removed.
   713	func (p Path) TrimLeadingSlash() *Path {
   714	        p.trimLeadingSlash = true
   715	        return &p
   716	}
   717	
   718	func (p *Path) norm(s string) string {
   719	        if p.trimLeadingSlash {
   720	                s = strings.TrimPrefix(s, "/")
   721	        }
   722	        return s
   723	}

   725	// IdentifierBase satisfies identity.Identity.
   726	func (p *Path) IdentifierBase() string {
   727	        if p.Component() == files.ComponentFolderLayouts {
   728	                return p.Path()
   729	        }
   730	        return p.Base()
   731	}

   735	        return p.component
   736	}

   738	// Container returns the base name of the container directory for this path.
   739	func (p *Path) Container() string {
   740	        if p.posContainerLow == -1 {
   741	                return ""
   742	        }
   743	        return p.norm(p.s[p.posContainerLow : p.posContainerHigh-1])
   744	}

   746	func (p *Path) String() string {
   747	        if p == nil {
   748	                return "<nil>"
   749	        }
   750	        return p.Path()

   925	func (p *Path) Base() string {

   954	func (p *Path) base(preserveExt, isBundle bool) string {
   955	        if len(p.identifiersKnown) == 0 {
   956	                return p.norm(p.s)
   957	        }
   958	
   959	        if preserveExt && len(p.identifiersKnown) == 1 {
   960	                // Preserve extension.
   961	                return p.norm(p.s)
   962	        }
   963	
   964	        var high int
   965

   967	                high = p.posContainerHigh - 1
   968	        } else {
   969	                high = p.nameLowHigh().High
   970	        }
   971	
   972	        if high == 0 {
   973	                high++
   974	        }
   975	
   976	        if !preserveExt {
   977	                return p.norm(p.s[:high])
   978	        }
   979	
   980	        // For txt files etc. we want to preserve the extension.
   981	        id := p.identifiersKnown[0]
   982	
   983	        return p.norm(p.s[:high] + p.s[id.Low-1:id.High])
   984	}

   224	func (pp *PathParser) SitesMatrixFromPath(p *Path) sitesmatrix.VectorStore {
   225	        pp.init()
   226	        langs := p.Langs()
   227	        versions := p.Versions()
   228	        roles := p.Roles()
   229	        lang := p.Lang() // First or dot-based language.
   230	        // Cache by the full site-selection identity derived from the path:
   231	        // languages, selected language, versions, and roles.
   232	        cacheKey := strings.Join(langs, ",") + "/" + lang + "/" + strings.Join(versions, ",") + "|" + strings.Join(roles, ",")
   233	        v, _ := pp.sitesMatrixCache.GetOrCreate(cacheKey, func() (sitesmatrix.VectorStore, error) {
   234	                builder := sitesmatrix.NewIntSetsBuilder(pp.ConfiguredDimensions)
   235	                if len(langs) > 0 {
   236	                        for _, l := range langs {
   237	                                if idx, ok := pp.LanguageIndex[l]; ok {
   238	                                        builder.WithLanguageIndices(idx)
   239	                                }
   240	                        }
   241	                } else if lang != "" {
   242	                        if idx, ok := pp.LanguageIndex[lang]; ok {
   243	                                builder.WithLanguageIndices(idx)
   244	                        }
   245	                }
   246	                for _, version := range versions {
   247	                        if idx := pp.ConfiguredDimensions.ConfiguredVersions.ResolveIndex(version); idx >= 0 {
   248	                                builder.WithVersionIndices(idx)
   249	                        }
   250	                }
   251	                for _, role := range roles {
   252	                        if idx := pp.ConfiguredDimensions.ConfiguredRoles.ResolveIndex(role); idx >= 0 {
   253	                                builder.WithRoleIndices(idx)
   254	                        }
   255	                }
   256	
   257	                switch p.Component() {
   258	                case files.ComponentFolderContent:
   259	                        builder.WithDefaultsIfNotSet()
   260	                case files.ComponentFolderLayouts:
   261	                        builder.WithAllIfNotSet()
   262	                case files.ComponentFolderStatic:
   263	                        builder.WithDefaultsAndAllLanguagesIfNotSet()
   264	                }
   265	
   266	                return builder.Build(), nil
   267	        })
   268	
   269	        return v
   270	}

   281	        p := pp.parsePooled(c, s)

   287	        s = NormalizePathStringBasic(s)
   288	        p := getPath()

   290	        p, err := pp.doParse(c, s, p)
   291	        if err != nil {
   292	                panic(err)
   293	        }
   294	        return p
   295	}

   307	        p := &Path{}

   311	}

   313	func (pp *PathParser) parse(component, s string) (*Path, error) {
   314	        ss := NormalizePathStringBasic(s)
   315	
   316	        p, err := pp.doParse(component, ss, pp.newPath(component))
   317	        if err != nil {
   318	                return nil, err
   319	        }

   323	                // Preserve the original case for titles etc.

   325	                if err != nil {
   326	                        return nil, err
   327	                }
   328	        } else {
   329	                p.unnormalized = p
   330	        }

    43	func NewFileMeta() *FileMeta {
    44	        return &FileMeta{}
    45	}
    46	
    47	// A subset of modules.Module used to avoid circular dependencies.
    48	// Note that it's safe to type assert to the full modules.Module when needed.
    49	type Module interface {
    50	        // Returns the path to this module.
    51	        // This will either be the module path, e.g. "github.com/gohugoio/myshortcodes",
    52	        // or the path below your /theme folder, e.g. "mytheme".
    53	        Path() string
    54	
    55	        // Directory holding files for this module.
    56	        Dir() string
    57	
    58	        // Returns whether this is a Go Module.
    59	        IsGoMod() bool
    60	
    61	        // The module version.
    62	        Version() string
    63	}
    64	
    65	// FileMeta holds metadata about a file or directory.
    66	type FileMeta struct {
    67	        PathInfo *paths.Path
    68	        Name     string
    69	        Filename string
    70	
    71	        BaseDir       string
    72	        SourceRoot    string
    73	        Module        Module
    74	        ModuleOrdinal int
    75	        Component     string
    76	
    77	        Weight    int
    78	        IsProject bool
    79	        Watch     bool
    80	
    81	        // This file/directory  will be built for these sites.
    82	        SitesMatrix sitesmatrix.VectorStore
    83	
    84	        // This file/directory complements these other sites.
    85	        SitesComplements sitesmatrix.VectorStore
    86	
    87	        OpenFunc     func() (afero.File, error)
    88	        JoinStatFunc func(name string) (FileMetaInfo, error)
    89	
    90	        // Include only files or directories that match.
    91	        InclusionFilter *hglob.FilenameFilter
    92	
    93	        // Rename the name part of the file (not the directory).
    94	        // Returns the new name and a boolean indicating if the file
    95	        // should be included.
    96	        Rename func(name string, toFrom bool) (string, bool)
    97	}
    98	
    99	func (m *FileMeta) Copy() *FileMeta {
   100	        if m == nil {
   101	                return NewFileMeta()
   102	        }
   103	        c := *m
   104	        return &c
   105	}
   106	
   107	func (m *FileMeta) Merge(from *FileMeta) {
   108	        if m == nil || from == nil {
   109	                return
   110	        }
   111	        dstv := reflect.Indirect(reflect.ValueOf(m))
   112	        srcv := reflect.Indirect(reflect.ValueOf(from))
   113	
   114	        for i := range dstv.NumField() {
   115	                v := dstv.Field(i)
   116	                if !v.CanSet() {
   117	                        continue
   118	                }
   119	                if !hreflect.IsTruthfulValue(v) {
   120	                        v.Set(srcv.Field(i))
   121	                }
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        if m.InclusionFilter == nil {
   125	                m.InclusionFilter = from.InclusionFilter
   126	        }
   127	}
   128	
   129	func (f *FileMeta) Open() (afero.File, error) {
   130	        if f.OpenFunc == nil {
   131	                return nil, errors.New("OpenFunc not set")
   132	        }
   133	        return f.OpenFunc()
   134	}
   135	
   136	func (f *FileMeta) ReadAll() ([]byte, error) {
   137	        file, err := f.Open()
   138	        if err != nil {
   139	                return nil, err
   140	        }
   141	        defer file.Close()
   142	        return io.ReadAll(file)
   143	}
   144	
   145	func (f *FileMeta) JoinStat(name string) (FileMetaInfo, error) {
   146	        if f.JoinStatFunc == nil {
   147	                return nil, os.ErrNotExist
   148	        }
   149	        return f.JoinStatFunc(name)
   150	}
   151	
   152	func (m *FileMeta) ModulePath() string {
   153	        if m.Module == nil {
   154	                return ""
   155	        }
   156	        return m.Module.Path()
   157	}
   158	
   159	func (m *FileMeta) MatchSiteVectorCoarse(v sitesmatrix.Vector) bool {
   160	        language := v.Language()
   161	        if !(m.SitesMatrix.HasLanguage(language) || m.SitesComplements.HasLanguage(language)) {
   162	                return false
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        return m.MatchSiteVectorCoarseExcludeLanguage(v)
   166	}
   167	
   168	func (m *FileMeta) MatchSiteVectorCoarseExcludeLanguage(v sitesmatrix.Vector) bool {
   169	        version := v.Version()
   170	        if !(m.SitesMatrix.HasVersion(version) || m.SitesComplements.HasVersion(version)) {
   171	                return false
   172	        }
   173	
   174	        role := v.Role()
   175	        // lint:ignore S1008 preserve the symmetry from above.
   176	        if !(m.SitesMatrix.HasRole(role) || m.SitesComplements.HasRole(role)) {
   177	                return false
   178	        }
   179	
   180	        return true
   181	}
   182	
   183	type FileMetaInfo interface {
   184	        fs.DirEntry
   185	        MetaProvider
   186	
   187	        // This is a real hybrid as it also implements the fs.FileInfo interface.
   188	        FileInfoOptionals
   189	}
   190	
   191	type MetaProvider interface {
   192	        Meta() *FileMeta
   193	}
   194	
   195	type FileInfoOptionals interface {
   196	        Size() int64
   197	        Mode() fs.FileMode
   198	        ModTime() time.Time
   199	        Sys() any
   200	}
   201	
   202	type FileNameIsDir interface {
   203	        Name() string
   204	        IsDir() bool
   205	}
   206	
   207	type FileInfoProvider interface {
   208	        FileInfo() FileMetaInfo
   209	}

   211	// DirOnlyOps is a subset of the afero.File interface covering
   212	// the methods needed for directory operations.
   213	type DirOnlyOps interface {
   214	        io.Closer
   215	        Name() string
   216	        Readdir(count int) ([]os.FileInfo, error)
   217	        Readdirnames(n int) ([]string, error)
   218	        Stat() (os.FileInfo, error)
   219	}
   220	
   221	type dirEntryMeta struct {
   222	        fs.DirEntry
   223	        m *FileMeta
   224	
   225	        fi     fs.FileInfo
   226	        fiInit sync.Once
   227	}
   228	
   229	func (fi *dirEntryMeta) Meta() *FileMeta {
   230	        return fi.m
   231	}
   232	
   233	// Filename returns the full filename.
   234	func (fi *dirEntryMeta) Filename() string {
   235	        return fi.m.Filename
   236	}
   237	
   238	func (fi *dirEntryMeta) fileInfo() fs.FileInfo {
   239	        var err error
   240	        fi.fiInit.Do(func() {
   241	                fi.fi, err = fi.DirEntry.Info()
   242	        })
   243	        if err != nil {
   244	                panic(err)
   245	        }
   246	        return fi.fi
   247	}
   248	
   249	func (fi *dirEntryMeta) Size() int64 {
   250	        return fi.fileInfo().Size()
   251	}
   252	
   253	func (fi *dirEntryMeta) Mode() fs.FileMode {
   254	        return fi.fileInfo().Mode()
   255	}
   256	
   257	func (fi *dirEntryMeta) ModTime() time.Time {
   258	        return fi.fileInfo().ModTime()
   259	}

   360	func (f *componentFsDir) Readdirnames(count int) ([]string, error) {

   383	func (fs *componentFs) Open(name string) (afero.File, error) {
   384	        f, err := fs.Fs.Open(name)

   676	func (s *IntSets) setDimensionsFromOtherIfNotSet(other VectorIterator) {
   677	        if other == nil {
   678	                return
   679	        }
   680	        setLang := s.languages == nil
   681	        setVer := s.versions == nil
   682	        setRole := s.roles == nil
   683	
   684	        if !(setLang || setVer || setRole) {
   685	                return
   686	        }
   687	
   688	        other.ForEachVector(func(v Vector) bool {
   689	                if !s.HasVector(v) {
   690	                        s.setValuesInNilSets(v, setLang, setVer, setRole)
   691	                }
   692	                return true
   693	        })
   694	}
   695	
   696	func (s *IntSets) setValuesInNilSets(vec Vector, setLang, setVer, setRole bool) {
   697	        if setLang {
   698	                if s.languages == nil {
   699	                        s.languages = hmaps.NewOrderedIntSet()
   700	                }
   701	                s.languages.Set(vec.Language())
   702	        }
   703	        if setVer {
   704	                if s.versions == nil {
   705	                        s.versions = hmaps.NewOrderedIntSet()
   706	                }
   707	                s.versions.Set(vec.Version())
   708	        }
   709	
   710	        if setRole {
   711	                if s.roles == nil {
   712	                        s.roles = hmaps.NewOrderedIntSet()
   713	                }
   714	                s.roles.Set(vec.Role())
   715	        }
   716	}

   726	func (b *IntSetsBuilder) Build() *IntSets {
   727	        b.s.init()
   728	
   729	        if b.s.LenVectors() == 1 {
   730	                // Cache it or use the existing cached version, which will allow b.s to be GCed.
   731	                bb, _ := b.cfg.singleVectorStoreCache.GetOrCreate(b.s.VectorSample(), func() (*IntSets, error) {
   732	                        return b.s, nil
   733	                })
   734	                return bb
   735	        }
   736	        return b.s
   737	}

    29	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/common/types"
    30	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/hugofs/hglob"
    31	)
    32	
    33	var (
    34	        _ VectorStore            = &IntSets{}
    35	        _ VectorStore            = &vectorStoreMap{}
    36	        _ hashstructure.Hashable = &IntSets{}
    37	        _ hashstructure.Hashable = &vectorStoreMap{}
    38	)
    39	
    40	func newVectorStoreMap(cap int) *vectorStoreMap {
    41	        return &vectorStoreMap{
    42	                sets: make(Vectors, cap),
    43	                h:    &hashOnce{},
    44	        }
    45	}
    46	
    47	func newVectorStoreMapFromVectors(v Vectors) *vectorStoreMap {
    48	        return &vectorStoreMap{
    49	                sets: v,
    50	                h:    &hashOnce{},
    51	        }
    52	}
    53	
    54	// A vector store backed by a map.
    55	type vectorStoreMap struct {
    56	        sets Vectors
    57	        h    *hashOnce
    58	}
    59	
    60	func (s *vectorStoreMap) initHash() {
    61	        s.h.once.Do(func() {
    62	                var err error
    63	                s.h.hash, err = hashing.Hash(s.sets)
    64	                if err != nil {
    65	                        panic(fmt.Errorf("failed to calculate hash for MapVectorStore: %w", err))
    66	                }
    67	        })
    68	}
    69	
    70	func (s *vectorStoreMap) setVector(vec Vector) {
    71	        s.sets[vec] = struct{}{}
    72	}
    73	
    74	func (s *vectorStoreMap) KeysSorted() ([]int, []int, []int) {
    75	        var k0, k1, k2 []int
    76	        for v := range s.sets {
    77	                k0 = append(k0, v.Language())
    78	                k1 = append(k1, v.Version())
    79	                k2 = append(k2, v.Role())
    80	        }
    81	        sort.Ints(k0)
    82	        sort.Ints(k1)
    83	        sort.Ints(k2)
    84	        k0 = slices.Compact(k0)
    85	        k1 = slices.Compact(k1)
    86	        k2 = slices.Compact(k2)
    87	
    88	        return k0, k1, k2
    89	}
    90	
    91	func (s *vectorStoreMap) Hash() (uint64, error) {
    92	        s.initHash()
    93	        return s.h.hash, nil
    94	}
    95	
    96	func (s *vectorStoreMap) MustHash() uint64 {
    97	        i, _ := s.Hash()
    98	        return i
    99	}
   100	
   101	func (s *vectorStoreMap) HasVector(v Vector) bool {
   102	        if _, ok := s.sets[v]; ok {
   103	                return true
   104	        }
   105	        return false
   106	}
   107	
   108	func (s *vectorStoreMap) HasAnyVector(v VectorProvider) bool {
   109	        if v == nil || s.LenVectors() == 0 || v.LenVectors() == 0 {
   110	                return false
   111	        }
   112	
   113	        return !v.ForEachVector(func(vec Vector) bool {
   114	                if s.HasVector(vec) {
   115	                        return false // stop iteration
   116	                }
   117	                return true // continue iteration
   118	        })
   119	}
   120	
   121	func (s *vectorStoreMap) LenVectors() int {
   122	        return len(s.sets)
   123	}
   124	
   125	// Complement returns a new VectorStore that contains all vectors in s that are not in any of ss.
   126	func (s *vectorStoreMap) Complement(ss ...VectorProvider) VectorStore {
   127	        if len(ss) == 0 || (len(ss) == 1 && ss[0] == s) {
   128	                return nil
   129	        }
   130	
   131	        for _, v := range ss {
   132	                if v == s {
   133	                        var s *vectorStoreMap
   134	                        return s
   135	                }
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        result := newVectorStoreMap(36)
   139	
   140	        s.ForEachVector(func(vec Vector) bool {

    20	const (
    21	        // Dimensions in the Hugo build matrix.
    22	        // These can be used as indices into the Vector type.
    23	        Language int = iota
    24	        Version
    25	        Role
    26	)
    27	
    28	// Vector represents a site vector in the Hugo sites matrix from the three dimensions:
    29	// Language, Version and Role.
    30	// This is a fixed-size array for performance reasons (for one, it can be used as map key).
    31	type Vector [3]int
    32	
    33	// Compare returns -1 if v1 is less than v2, 0 if they are equal, and 1 if v1 is greater than v2.
    34	// This adds a implicit weighting to the dimensions, where the first dimension is the most important,
    35	// but this is just used for sorting to get stable output.
    36	func (v1 Vector) Compare(v2 Vector) int {
    37	        // note that a and b will never be equal.
    38	        minusOneOrOne := func(a, b int) int {
    39	                if a < b {
    40	                        return -1
    41	                }
    42	                return 1
    43	        }
    44	        if v1[0] != v2[0] {
    45	                return minusOneOrOne(v1[0], v2[0])
    46	        }
    47	        if v1[1] != v2[1] {
    48	                return minusOneOrOne(v1[1], v2[1])
    49	        }
    50	        if v1[2] != v2[2] {
    51	                return minusOneOrOne(v1[2], v2[2])
    52	        }
    53	        // They are equal.
    54	        return 0
    55	}
    56	
    57	// Distance returns the distance between v1 and v2
    58	// using the first dimension that is different.
    59	func (v1 Vector) Distance(v2 Vector) int {
    60	        if v1[0] != v2[0] {
    61	                return v1[0] - v2[0]
    62	        }
    63	        if v1[1] != v2[1] {
    64	                return v1[1] - v2[1]
    65	        }
    66	        if v1[2] != v2[2] {
    67	                return v1[2] - v2[2]
    68	        }
    69	        return 0
    70	}
    71	
    72	// EuclideanDistanceSquared returns the Euclidean distance between two vectors as the sum of the squared differences.
    73	
    74	func (v1 Vector) HasVector(v2 Vector) bool {
    75	        return v1 == v2
    76	}
    77	
    78	func (v1 Vector) HasAnyVector(vp VectorProvider) bool {
    79	        n := vp.LenVectors()
    80	        if n == 0 {
    81	                return false
    82	        }
    83	        if n == 1 {
    84	                return v1 == vp.VectorSample()
    85	        }
    86	
    87	        return !vp.ForEachVector(func(v2 Vector) bool {
    88	                if v1 == v2 {
    89	                        return false // stop iteration
    90	                }
    91	                return true // continue iteration
    92	        })
    93	}
    94	
    95	func (v1 Vector) LenVectors() int {
    96	        return 1
    97	}
    98	
    99	func (v1 Vector) VectorSample() Vector {
   100	        return v1
   101	}
   102	
   103	func (v1 Vector) EqualsVector(other VectorProvider) bool {
   104	        if other.LenVectors() != 1 {
   105	                return false
   106	        }
   107	        return other.VectorSample() == v1
   108	}
   109	
   110	func (v1 Vector) ForEachVector(yield func(v Vector) bool) bool {
   111	        return yield(v1)
   112	}

   115	func (v1 Vector) Language() int {
   116	        return v1[Language]
   117	}

   450	func (s *IntSets) VectorSample() Vector {
   451	        if s.LenVectors() == 0 {
   452	                panic("no vectors available")
   453	        }
   454	
   455	        return Vector{
   456	                s.languages.Next(0),
   457	                s.versions.Next(0),
   458	                s.roles.Next(0),
   459	        }
   460	}
   461	
   462	// The reason we don't use iter.Seq is https://github.com/golang/go/issues/69015
   463	// This is 60% faster and allocation free.
   464	// The yield function should return false to stop iteration.
   465	func (s *IntSets) ForEachVector(yield func(v Vector) bool) bool {
   466	        if s.LenVectors() == 0 {
   467	                return true
   468	        }
   469	
   470	        b := s.languages.ForEachKey(func(lang int) bool {
   471	                return s.versions.ForEachKey(func(ver int) bool {
   472	                        return s.roles.ForEachKey(func(role int) bool {
   473	                                return yield(Vector{lang, ver, role})
   474	                        })
   475	                })
   476	        })
   477	
   478	        return b
   479	}
   480	
   481	func (s *IntSets) Vectors() []Vector {
   482	        if s.LenVectors() == 0 {
   483	                return nil
   484	        }
   485	
   486	        var vectors []Vector
   487	        s.ForEachVector(func(v Vector) bool {
   488	                vectors = append(vectors, v)
   489	                return true
   490	        })
   491	
   492	        sort.Slice(vectors, func(i, j int) bool {
   493	                v1, v2 := vectors[i], vectors[j]
   494	                return v1.Compare(v2) < 0
   495	        })
   496	
   497	        return vectors
   498	}
   499	
   500	func (s *IntSets) KeysSorted() ([]int, []int, []int) {
   501	        if s == nil {
   502	                return nil, nil, nil
   503	        }
   504	        languages := s.languages.KeysSorted()
   505	        versions := s.versions.KeysSorted()
   506	        roles := s.roles.KeysSorted()
   507	        return languages, versions, roles
   508	}
   509	
   510	func (s *IntSets) HasLanguage(lang int) bool {
   511	        if s == nil {
   512	                return false
   513	        }
   514	        return s.languages.Has(lang)
   515	}
   516	
   517	// LenVectors returns the total number of vectors represented by the IntSets.
   518	// This is the Cartesian product of the lengths of the individual sets.
   519	// This will be 0 if s is nil or any of the sets is empty.
   520	func (s *IntSets) LenVectors() int {
   521	        if s == nil {
   522	                return 0
   523	        }
   524	        return s.languages.Len() * s.versions.Len() * s.roles.Len()
   525	}
   526	
   527	func (s *IntSets) HasRole(role int) bool {
   528	        if s == nil {
   529	                return false
   530	        }
   531	        return s.roles.Has(role)
   532	}
   533	
   534	func (s *IntSets) String() string {
   535	        return fmt.Sprintf("Languages: %v, Versions: %v, Roles: %v", s.languages, s.versions, s.roles)
   536	}

   538	// HasVector checks if the given vector is contained in the sets.
   539	func (s *IntSets) HasVector(v Vector) bool {
   540	        if s == nil {
   541	                return false
   542	        }
   543	        if !s.languages.Has(v.Language()) {
   544	                return false
   545	        }
   546	        if !s.versions.Has(v.Version()) {
   547	                return false
   548	        }
   549	        if !s.roles.Has(v.Role()) {
   550	                return false
   551	        }
   552	        return true
   553	}

   196	
   197	func (s *vectorStoreMap) Vectors() []Vector {
   198	        if s == nil || len(s.sets) == 0 {
   199	                return nil
   200	        }
   201	        var vectors []Vector
   202	        for v := range s.sets {
   203	                vectors = append(vectors, v)
   204	        }
   205	        sort.Slice(vectors, func(i, j int) bool {
   206	                v1, v2 := vectors[i], vectors[j]
   207	                return v1.Compare(v2) < 0
   208	        })
   209	        return vectors
   210	}
   211	
   212	func (s *vectorStoreMap) WithLanguageIndices(i int) VectorStore {
   213	        c := s.clone()
   214	
   215	        for v := range c.sets {
   216	                v[Language] = i
   217	                c.sets[v] = struct{}{}
   218	        }
   219	
   220	        return c
   221	}

   461	func TestFileMountSitesMatrixResourcesRoles(t *testing.T) {
   462	        filesTemplate := `
   463	-- hugo.toml --
   464	disableKinds = ["taxonomy", "term", "rss", "sitemap", "section"]
   465	defaultContentRole = "guest"
   466	defaultContentRoleInSubDir = true

   470	[roles.member]
   471	weight = 200
   472	[mounts]
   473	[[module.mounts]]
   474	source = 'content/guest'
   475	target = 'content'
   476	[module.mounts.sites.matrix]
   477	roles = "guest"
   478	[[module.mounts]]
   479	source = 'content/member'
   480	target = 'content'
   481	[module.mounts.sites.matrix]
   482	roles = "member"
   483	-- layouts/all.html --
   484	{{ .Title }}|{{ .RelPermalink }}|Resources: {{ range .Resources }}{{ .RelPermalink }}|{{ end }}$
   485	-- content/guest/p1/index.md --
   486	---
   487	title: "Guest Gallery"
   488	---
   489	-- content/member/p1/index.md --
   490	---
   491	title: "Member Gallery"
   492	---
   493	-- content/guest/p1/mytext.txt --

   497	
   498	`

   500	        t.Run("Issue 1", func(t *testing.T) {
   501	                t.Parallel()
   502	                files := strings.Replace(filesTemplate, "content/member/p1/index.md", "content/member/p1_removed/index.md", 1)
   503	                files = strings.Replace(files, `roles = "guest"`, `roles = "*"`, 1)
   504	                b := hugolib.Test(t, files)
   505	
   506	                // The current behavior is well intended: We avoid copying the same resources to multiple places.
   507	                // But for the typical role use case, this typically leads to 404 errors for shared resources in the member section.
   508	                b.AssertFileContent("public/guest/p1/index.html", "Guest Gallery|/guest/p1/|Resources: /guest/p1/mytext.txt|/guest/p1/mytext2.txt|$")
   509	                b.AssertFileContent("public/member/p1/index.html", "Guest Gallery|/member/p1/|Resources: /member/p1/mytext.txt|/member/p1/mytext2.txt|$")
   510	        })
   511	
   512	        t.Run("Issue 2", func(t *testing.T) {
   513	                t.Parallel()
   514	                files := filesTemplate
   515	                b := hugolib.Test(t, files)
   516	
   517	                // This comes from how we handled languages before we added version and role:
   518	                // You would typically add 1 image resources and then translate the markdown files to multiple languages.
   519	                // To make sure that all languages got a complete set when doing Page.Resources, we pull in missing resources from, in this case, the member section.
   520	                // This obviously doesn't work for the role dimension, but it works for the language dimension, and we need to make sure that we don't break that.

   334	
   335	func (pp *PathParser) parseIdentifier(component, s string, p *Path, i, lastDot, numDots int, isLast bool) {
   336	        if p.posContainerHigh != -1 {
   337	                return
   338	        }
   339	        mayHaveLang := numDots > 1 && p.posIdentifierLanguage == -1 && pp.LanguageIndex != nil
   340	        mayHaveLang = mayHaveLang && (component == files.ComponentFolderContent || component == files.ComponentFolderLayouts)
   341	        mayHaveOutputFormat := component == files.ComponentFolderLayouts
   342	        mayHaveKind := p.posIdentifierKind == -1 && mayHaveOutputFormat
   343	        var mayHaveLayout bool
   344	        if p.pathType == TypeShortcode {
   345	                mayHaveLayout = !isLast && component == files.ComponentFolderLayouts
   346	        } else {
   347	                mayHaveLayout = component == files.ComponentFolderLayouts
   348	        }
   349	
   350	        var found bool
   351	        var high int
   352	        if len(p.identifiersKnown) > 0 {
   353	                high = lastDot
   354	        } else {
   355	                high = len(p.s)
   356	        }
   357	        id := types.LowHigh[string]{Low: i + 1, High: high}
   358	        sid := p.s[id.Low:id.High]
   359	
   360	        if isCustomWrapperIdentifier(sid) {
   361	                inner := sid[1 : len(sid)-1]
   362	                if prefix := parsePrefixIdentifier(inner); prefix != "" {
   363	                        // Value-only LowHigh: skip leading _ + prefix, trailing _
   364	                        valueID := types.LowHigh[string]{Low: id.Low + 1 + len(prefix), High: id.High - 1}
   365	                        if pp.applyPrefixIdentifier(component, prefix, p, valueID) {
   366	                                found = true
   367	                        }
   368	                }
   369	                if !found {
   370	                        p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   371	                        p.posIdentifierCustom = len(p.identifiersKnown) - 1
   372	                        found = true
   373	                }
   374	        }
   375	
   376	        if found {
   377	                // Already handled (e.g. prefix wrapper).
   378	        } else if len(p.identifiersKnown) == 0 {
   379	                // The first is always the extension.
   380	                p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   381	                found = true
   382	
   383	                // May also be the output format.
   384	                if mayHaveOutputFormat && pp.IsOutputFormat(sid, "") {
   385	                        p.posIdentifierOutputFormat = 0
   386	                }
   387	        } else {
   388	                var langFound bool
   389	
   390	                if mayHaveLang {
   391	                        var disabled bool
   392	                        _, langFound = pp.LanguageIndex[sid]
   393	
   394	                        if !langFound {
   395	                                disabled = pp.IsLangDisabled != nil && pp.IsLangDisabled(sid)
   396	                                if disabled {
   397	                                        p.disabled = true
   398	                                        langFound = true
   399	                                }
   400	                        }
   401	                        found = langFound
   402	                        if langFound {
   403	                                p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   404	                                p.posIdentifierLanguage = len(p.identifiersKnown) - 1
   405	                        }
   406	
   407	                }
   408	
   409	                if !found && mayHaveOutputFormat {
   410	                        // At this point we may already have resolved an output format,
   411	                        // but we need to keep looking for a more specific one, e.g. amp before html.
   412	                        // Use both name and extension to prevent
   413	                        // false positives on the form css.html.
   414	                        if pp.IsOutputFormat(sid, p.Ext()) {
   415	                                found = true
   416	                                p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   417	                                p.posIdentifierOutputFormat = len(p.identifiersKnown) - 1
   418	                        }
   419	                }
   420	
   421	                if !found && mayHaveKind {
   422	                        if kinds.GetKindMain(sid) != "" {
   423	                                found = true
   424	                                p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   425	                                p.posIdentifierKind = len(p.identifiersKnown) - 1
   426	                        }
   427	                }
   428	
   429	                if !found && sid == identifierBaseof {
   430	                        found = true
   431	                        p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   432	                        p.posIdentifierBaseof = len(p.identifiersKnown) - 1
   433	                }
   434	
   435	                if !found && mayHaveLayout {
   436	                        if p.posIdentifierLayout != -1 {
   437	                                // Move it to identifiersUnknown.
   438	                                p.identifiersUnknown = append(p.identifiersUnknown, p.identifiersKnown[p.posIdentifierLayout])
   439	                                p.identifiersKnown[p.posIdentifierLayout] = id
   440	                        } else {
   441	                                p.identifiersKnown = append(p.identifiersKnown, id)
   442	                                p.posIdentifierLayout = len(p.identifiersKnown) - 1
   443	                        }
   444	                        found = true
   445	                }
   446	
   447	                if !found {
   448	                        p.identifiersUnknown = append(p.identifiersUnknown, id)
   449	                }
   450	
   451	        }
   452	
   453	        if found {
   454	                if isLast {
   455	                        // The isLast identifier starts right at the container boundary.
   456	                        // Treat it as part of the name (e.g. layout name "list" in list.no.html).
   457	                        if p.posNameHigh <= 0 {
   458	                                p.posNameHigh = lastDot
   459	                        }
   460	                } else {
   461	                        p.posNameHigh = i // The '.' before this identifier.
   462	                }
   463	        }
   464	}
   465	
   466	func (pp *PathParser) doParse(component, s string, p *Path) (*Path, error) {
   467	        if runtime.GOOS == "windows" {
   468	                s = path.Clean(filepath.ToSlash(s))
   469	                if s == "." {
   470	                        s = ""

package sitesmatrix_test

import (
    "testing"
    "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/hugolib"
)

func TestReproFilenameRoleOverridesMountRole(t *testing.T) {
    files := `
-- hugo.toml --
disableKinds = ["taxonomy", "term", "rss", "sitemap", "home"]
defaultContentRole = "guest"
defaultContentRoleInSubDir = true
[roles]
[roles.guest]
weight = 100
[roles.member]
weight = 200
[[module.mounts]]
source = 'content/member'
target = 'content'
[module.mounts.sites.matrix]
roles = "member"
[[module.mounts]]
source = 'content/guest'
target = 'content'
[module.mounts.sites.matrix]
roles = "*"
-- layouts/section.html --
{{ .Title }}|{{ .RelPermalink }}|Resources: {{ range .Resources }}{{ .Name }}|{{ end }}$
-- content/member/p1/_index.md --
---
title: Member
---
-- content/guest/p1/_index.md --
---
title: Guest
---
-- content/guest/p1/memberonly._role_member_.txt --
Member only
-- content/guest/p1/common.txt --
Common
`
    b := hugolib.Test(t, files)
    b.AssertFileContent("public/guest/p1/index.html", "Guest|/guest/p1/|Resources: common.txt|$")
    b.AssertFileContent("public/member/p1/index.html", "Member|/member/p1/|Resources: common.txt|memberonly._role_member_.txt|$")
}
EOF
cp /tmp/repro_sitesmatrix_test.go hugolib/sitesmatrix/repro_tmp_test.go
go test ./hugolib/sitesmatrix -run TestReproFilenameRoleOverridesMountRole -count=1
status=$?
rm hugolib/sitesmatrix/repro_tmp_test.go
exit $status

func replaceSiteMatrixDimensions(vs sitesmatrix.VectorStore, languages, versions, roles []int) sitesmatrix.VectorStore {
	if vs == nil || (len(languages) == 0 && len(versions) == 0 && len(roles) == 0) {
		return vs
	}

	vectors := make(sitesmatrix.Vectors)
	vs.ForEachVector(func(v sitesmatrix.Vector) bool {
		for _, language := range valuesOrCurrent(languages, v.Language()) {
			for _, version := range valuesOrCurrent(versions, v.Version()) {
				for _, role := range valuesOrCurrent(roles, v.Role()) {
					vectors[sitesmatrix.Vector{language, version, role}] = struct{}{}
				}
			}
		}
		return true
	})

	return vectors.ToVectorStore()
}

func valuesOrCurrent(values []int, current int) []int {
	if len(values) == 0 {
		return []int{current}
	}
	return values
}

package sitesmatrix_test

import (
    "testing"
    "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/hugolib"
)

func TestReproFilenameRoleOverridesMountRole(t *testing.T) {
    files := `
-- hugo.toml --
disableKinds = ["taxonomy", "term", "rss", "sitemap", "home"]
defaultContentRole = "guest"
defaultContentRoleInSubDir = true
[roles]
[roles.guest]
weight = 100
[roles.member]
weight = 200
[[module.mounts]]
source = 'content/member'
target = 'content'
[module.mounts.sites.matrix]
roles = "member"
[[module.mounts]]
source = 'content/guest'
target = 'content'
[module.mounts.sites.matrix]
roles = "*"
-- layouts/section.html --
{{ .Title }}|{{ .RelPermalink }}|Resources: {{ range .Resources }}{{ .Name }}|{{ end }}$
-- content/member/p1/_index.md --
---
title: Member
---
-- content/guest/p1/_index.md --
---
title: Guest
---
-- content/guest/p1/memberonly._role_member_.txt --
Member only
-- content/guest/p1/common.txt --
Common
`
    b := hugolib.Test(t, files)
    b.AssertFileContent("public/guest/p1/index.html", "Guest|/guest/p1/|Resources: common.txt|$")
    b.AssertFileContent("public/member/p1/index.html", "Member|/member/p1/|Resources: common.txt|memberonly._role_member_.txt|$")
}
EOF
cp /tmp/repro_sitesmatrix_test.go hugolib/sitesmatrix/repro_tmp_test.go
go test ./hugolib/sitesmatrix -run TestReproFilenameRoleOverridesMountRole -count=1
status=$?
rm hugolib/sitesmatrix/repro_tmp_test.go
exit $status

    33	
    34	func replaceSiteMatrixDimensions(vs sitesmatrix.VectorStore, languages, versions, roles []int) sitesmatrix.VectorStore {
    35	        if vs == nil || (len(languages) == 0 && len(versions) == 0 && len(roles) == 0) {
    36	                return vs
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        vectors := make(sitesmatrix.Vectors)
    40	        vs.ForEachVector(func(v sitesmatrix.Vector) bool {
    41	                for _, language := range valuesOrCurrent(languages, v.Language()) {
    42	                        for _, version := range valuesOrCurrent(versions, v.Version()) {
    43	                                for _, role := range valuesOrCurrent(roles, v.Role()) {
    44	                                        vectors[sitesmatrix.Vector{language, version, role}] = struct{}{}
    45	                                }
    46	                        }
    47	                }
    48	                return true
    49	        })
    50	
    51	        return vectors.ToVectorStore()
    52	}
    53	
    54	func valuesOrCurrent(values []int, current int) []int {
    55	        if len(values) == 0 {
    56	                return []int{current}
    57	        }
    58	        return values
    59	}
    60

    63	        if opts.Component == "" {
    64	                panic("ComponentFsOptions.PathParser.Component must be set")
    65	        }

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/repro_sitesmatrix_test.go <<'EOF'
package sitesmatrix_test

import (
    "testing"
    "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/hugolib"
)

func TestReproFilenameRoleOverridesMountRole(t *testing.T) {
    files := `
-- hugo.toml --
disableKinds = ["taxonomy", "term", "rss", "sitemap", "home"]
defaultContentRole = "guest"
defaultContentRoleInSubDir = true
[roles]
[roles.guest]
weight = 100
[roles.member]
weight = 200
[[module.mounts]]
source = 'content/member'
target = 'content'
[module.mounts.sites.matrix]
roles = "member"
[[module.mounts]]
source = 'content/guest'
target = 'content'
[module.mounts.sites.matrix]
roles = "*"
-- layouts/section.html --
{{ .Title }}|{{ .RelPermalink }}|Resources: {{ range .Resources }}{{ .Name }}|{{ end }}$
-- content/member/p1/_index.md --
---
title: Member
---
-- content/guest/p1/_index.md --
---
title: Guest
---
-- content/guest/p1/memberonly._role_member_.txt --
Member only
-- content/guest/p1/common.txt --
Common
`
    b := hugolib.Test(t, files)
    b.AssertFileContent("public/guest/p1/index.html", "Guest|/guest/p1/|Resources: common.txt|$")
    b.AssertFileContent("public/member/p1/index.html", "Member|/member/p1/|Resources: common.txt|memberonly._role_member_.txt|$")
}
EOF
cp /tmp/repro_sitesmatrix_test.go hugolib/sitesmatrix/repro_tmp_test.go
go test ./hugolib/sitesmatrix -run TestReproFilenameRoleOverridesMountRole -count=1
status=$?
rm hugolib/sitesmatrix/repro_tmp_test.go
exit $status

+func replaceSiteMatrixDimensions(vs sitesmatrix.VectorStore, languages, versions, roles []int) sitesmatrix.VectorStore {
+	if vs == nil || (len(languages) == 0 && len(versions) == 0 && len(roles) == 0) {
+		return vs
+	}
+
+	vectors := make(sitesmatrix.Vectors)
+	vs.ForEachVector(func(v sitesmatrix.Vector) bool {
+		for _, language := range valuesOrCurrent(languages, v.Language()) {
+			for _, version := range valuesOrCurrent(versions, v.Version()) {
+				for _, role := range valuesOrCurrent(roles, v.Role()) {
+					vectors[sitesmatrix.Vector{language, version, role}] = struct{}{}
+				}
+			}
+		}
+		return true
+	})
+
+	return vectors.ToVectorStore()
+}
+
+func valuesOrCurrent(values []int, current int) []int {
+	if len(values) == 0 {
+		return []int{current}
+	}
+	return values
+}

package sitesmatrix_test

import (
    "testing"
    "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/hugolib"
)

func TestReproFilenameRoleOverridesMountRole(t *testing.T) {
    files := `
-- hugo.toml --
disableKinds = ["taxonomy", "term", "rss", "sitemap", "home"]
defaultContentRole = "guest"
defaultContentRoleInSubDir = true
[roles]
[roles.guest]
weight = 100
[roles.member]
weight = 200
[[module.mounts]]
source = 'content/member'
target = 'content'
[module.mounts.sites.matrix]
roles = "member"
[[module.mounts]]
source = 'content/guest'
target = 'content'
[module.mounts.sites.matrix]
roles = "*"
-- layouts/section.html --
{{ .Title }}|{{ .RelPermalink }}|Resources: {{ range .Resources }}{{ .Name }}|{{ end }}$
-- content/member/p1/_index.md --
---
title: Member
---
-- content/guest/p1/_index.md --
---
title: Guest
---
-- content/guest/p1/memberonly._role_member_.txt --
Member only
-- content/guest/p1/common.txt --
Common
`
    b := hugolib.Test(t, files)
    b.AssertFileContent("public/guest/p1/index.html", "Guest|/guest/p1/|Resources: common.txt|$")
    b.AssertFileContent("public/member/p1/index.html", "Member|/member/p1/|Resources: common.txt|memberonly._role_member_.txt|$")
}
EOF
cp /tmp/repro_sitesmatrix_test.go hugolib/sitesmatrix/repro_tmp_test.go

2026-05-30 05:25:05,830 - INFO - swea-agent-gohugoio__hugo-14757 - Found submission: diff --git a/hugofs/component_fs.go b/hugofs/component_fs.go

 	"golang.org/x/text/unicode/norm"
 )
 
+func replaceSiteMatrixDimensions(vs sitesmatrix.VectorStore, languages, versions, roles []int) sitesmatrix.VectorStore {
+	if vs == nil || (len(languages) == 0 && len(versions) == 0 && len(roles) == 0) {
+		return vs
+	}
+
+	vectors := make(sitesmatrix.Vectors)
+	vs.ForEachVector(func(v sitesmatrix.Vector) bool {
+		for _, language := range valuesOrCurrent(languages, v.Language()) {
+			for _, version := range valuesOrCurrent(versions, v.Version()) {
+				for _, role := range valuesOrCurrent(roles, v.Role()) {
+					vectors[sitesmatrix.Vector{language, version, role}] = struct{}{}
+				}
+			}
+		}
+		return true
+	})
+
+	return vectors.ToVectorStore()
+}
+
+func valuesOrCurrent(values []int, current int) []int {
+	if len(values) == 0 {
+		return []int{current}
+	}
+	return values
+}
+
